class="media__icon icon-media-video" data-post-text="03:12"></i></a></div><div class="cd__content"><h3 class="cd__headline"  data-analytics="%20(58%20Videos)_carousel-medium-strip_video_video"><a href="/videos/politics/2016/01/17/trump-cruz-jabs-mj-lee-lklv.cnn/video/playlists/donald-trump/" ><span class="cd__headline-text">Donald Trump booed for attacking Ted Cruz</span><span class="cd__headline-icon"></span></a></h3></div></div></article></div></div></div></div></div></section></div><div class="pg-rail-tall__body" itemprop="articleBody"><section class="zn zn-body-text zn-body zn--idx-0 zn-has-multiple-containers zn-has-16-containers" data-eq-pts="xsmall: 0, medium: 460, large: 780, full16x9: 1100" id="body-text" data-vr-zone="zone-1-0" data-zone-label="bodyText" data-containers="16" id="body-text" data-zn-id="body-text"><div class="l-container"><div class="el__leafmedia el__leafmedia--sourced-paragraph"><p class="zn-body__paragraph"><cite class="el-editorial-source"> (CNN)</cite>Responding to a volley of critical tweets and comments from Jeb Bush, Donald Trump on Monday called his rival -- the son of one president and brother of another -- an "embarrassment to his family."</p></div><p class="zn-body__paragraph">Moments earlier, Bush<a href="http://cnn.it/1Q5lR65" target="_blank"> told </a>CNN's Dana Bash he was a "joyful warrior," who wouldn't sit back and watch "someone try to hijack a party that I believe will allow people to rise up again." </p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">Trump, who had been watching Bush's interview, fired back immediately, launching a series of aggressive attacks and insults at the former Florida governor.</p><div class="ad ad--epic ad--mobile" data-ad-text="show"><div id="ad_rect_btf_02" class="ad-ad_rect_btf_02 ad-refresh-default"></div></div><ul class="cn cn-list-hierarchical-xs cn--idx-4 cn-zoneAdContainer"></ul><p class="zn-body__paragraph">"Jeb is having some kind of a breakdown," he told CNN's Wolf Blitzer. â€‹"He's an embarrassment to his family. He has to bring his mother out and walk his mother around at 90 years old. I think it's a very sad situation that's taking place."</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">"Frankly, he's a stiff," Trump said. "He's not a guy who can be president. He doesn't have what it takes to be president."</p><div class="zn-body__read-more"><div class="read-more-gradient"></div><div class="read-more-button"><div class="read-more-link" id="js-body-read-more">Read More</div></div></div><div class="zn-body__read-all"><p class="zn-body__paragraph">Barbara Bush, Jeb's mother, recently <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/02/05/politics/barbara-bush-jeb-bush-donald-trump/">joined her son</a> on the campaign trail in New Hampshire, where the former first lady ripped Trump, saying she was "sick of him" and "not crazy about what he says about women."</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">Trump, though, kept his focus trained on Jeb Bush.</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">"He's a desperate person. He's a sad and a pathetic person. He doesn't even use his last name in his ad," Trump said, asked to react to a tweet Bush's campaign sent out earlier calling him a "loser" and a "liar." "He's a sad person who has gone absolutely crazy. I mean, this guy is a nervous wreck."</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">The billionaire also swatted away Bush's claim to being the only GOP candidate willing to stand toe-to-toe with Trump on the debate stage.</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">"[Bush] goes around saying, 'I'm the only one with the courage to go after Trump.' What courage is it?," Trump asked. "He says nasty things and I put him down on the dais and he goes away like a little sheep."</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">Trump also dismissed Bush's assertions that, despite their primary fight, he and former colleague and protege Marco Rubio were still "friends."</p><p class="zn-body__paragraph">"He hates Rubio so much, he can't stand the sight of him," Trump said, adding that Bush believes Rubio "violated the friendship" by deciding to run for the Republican nomination.</p></div><p class="zn-body__paragraph zn-body__footer"></p></div><div class="zn-body__read-more-outbrain"><ul class="cn cn-list-hierarchical-small-horizontal cn--idx-0 cn-"><li><article class="cd cd--tool cd--tool__outbrain" data-analytics="tool-type_list-hierarchical-small-horizontal_outbrain"
